et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	If the wound remains open and does not close up properly, and you find an abscess between your finger and the wound, cover it with a thick layer of lard or syrup, and watch the abscess that is under the covering to see if it bursts.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the head of the fistula at its beginning, presses immediately against the tent, and then apply the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	The tent will be opened and cut; then take the charr fatries that seem like a bird's feather, and none remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the wound is gaping, and cuts between you and the incision, cauterize it with fire or medicine ointment.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	Fire cauteries bring together two good things: the burning of these attached charms, and the stopping of blood flow and the drying out of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of wet tents in butter or crushed cheeses, until the lees settle down, and the charms are burned in the butter.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with onion juice made of hard charcoal, and the medicine is dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	When it is treated, it becomes healed and does not return again.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes up to the full depth of the foundation, and is removed from the body, push your finger or foundation in there and check it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the membrane or fabric or flesh that is about to pierce, but there is no way out except through hope and faith from the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you plunge it to the bottom, or if it is pus-filled, you pierce it and heal it as we did earlier.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And go not too deep, lest you cover the holding device that supports the base, and let the evacuation come by its own will.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then heal, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	If it happens to be sound, then remove the covering and clean it once it is removed from its base, either by stretching or by using some instrument pointed for that purpose.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then disinfect the wound with the charred material to the extent possible;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then study to heal the wound, and keep the fistula in the part outside of its base; it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes are fistulas in this manner: and it is when you press the tent [or probe] into the fistula, and it is where it touches the base of the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	If you take a probing stick at its tip in this manner:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And insert one thick thread into two, and push the sheath all the way to the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is perforated at the margin of the foundation within, then draw out the thread from the perforation, thus you push your hand or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And draw out the thread from the tip of the fistula, and bring together the two heads, and bind one to the other, and leave for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And hold it without movement, until the threads catch these charms that are between them, and pierce.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce itself, then make it pierce in every possible way, as long as it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it should not be covered with a plaster that goes too deep, and then healed as we have said, until it is healthy.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of a spur-like thorn with which they make a fistula is very sharp at one end and cuts through.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand not, because one should not strike where one should not strike, as you see here:
des emorroydes	hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two types. The first type is located inside the foundation, like a piece of resin, and there are small and large ones, and in the outside it has blood.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	And if there are one or more (of them), and they are dislocated from their foundation and at the base of the foundation; but those that are dislocated have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	And furthermore there is also some citron-yellow liquid or blood, and they have the color of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the cure for those who have them within the foundation is that you command the patient to strain themselves to urinate in a chamber, until the foundation settles down and this can be seen by the sons.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, hold it with pliers or grip it with your nail, then strike its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if they cannot be held by pliers due to moisture, take a cloth or cotton, or a piece of gauze instead.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	hold it with your hands, then strike and sprinkle some hot powders instead of cautery on top.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize it as the chapter on cautery says, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundation cannot come out, clisterize the patient with biting and sharp clistere to clean the area where the foundation is, so that it may come out openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patients prepare themselves, and if their threads are deep in the foundation, then the treatment will be easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grasp them with your nail or tweezers, strike them, and then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary to apply the suturing in this manner: take one twisted thread and put it on a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread below the needle.  This will be continued until the wound has been completely closed.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And if it is wide (the wound); draw the thread out, then tie it, and draw out the needle, and do the same with all the others, and leave one for draining excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the foundation a moist cloth soaked in rose oil or pitch, and place it on the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then leave it until it stops bleeding, and when it has stopped, treat the wound with salve and other remedies until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	The drying of wounds or foundations
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often there is drying of wounds in the intestines due to natural constraint and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you press with the tip of a spatula or your nail the scab above it, so as not to let it get wet.

puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then let it heal as long as it is healed.
dou fremit	toothache.
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A formice is a small creature that burrows near the body and moves forward a lot.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the fever strikes the throat, and it feels like death by shivering, and it affects the whole body, more in the hands than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is to take a cane made of goose feather or strong hen feather and place it around the shivering, until the purple circles it all over;   Et tu fais le cierge ou il soit adoussi a la couleur de sanc, et mette l’autre cainne sur li, qui soit adousse à la couleur de vermeil, et maintiens ce li cierges tant que les coulours estrent jaunis et le fremit est desaussiez.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand all around the cane until you cover it completely over the shivering, and put it inside, and dry out the shivering from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see (it), do as follows with a cat of oil or iron in this manner, and make it thin underneath and draw it out from above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not perforate, as it is to maintain the tooth, and press more; and if you see (it), cauterize the pain, as it is in front or chapter of cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of the clyster   This sentence does not have a direct translation equivalent to English, but "clistere" refers to an enema or rectal irrigation, and "de la forme" means "of the shape". The context suggests that the author is referring to the instrument used for this procedure.
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes a silver or copper clyster, or melted tallow or oil, is made; and sometimes these small or large instruments are made, depending on the ones brought to hand.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, those to be treated in children's care and who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the cupping glass can be both small and large, or the abdomen is bound in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and it should have an opening where the abdomen is bound, as you can see, and the chest should be pierced on two sides, one with two holes and the other with one;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	And let the stomach or a man put the medicine from a beast's bladder or parchment, and it should be pierced all around with small holes.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and there should be space between each hole, then insert a strong thread through each hole, around ten or more around, and bind the stomach like a goatskin.

Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head with caster oil or goose fat, or something similar, then gently apply it;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	then the ministers should press it with their two hands together until it is all visible, then remove the caster oil, and wash the patient's legs.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	if the medicine seems to come out, squeeze it as much as possible; and if it sleeps for an entire night, it is more helpful.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cauterize in the disease of belly decay, and the medicine is quick to heal, continue it until it is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are foundation or abscess, then use the clyster as gentle as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	this is the form of the gentle clyster on which the skin should be stretched:
des plaies	wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have said in the division the treatment of wounds; now we will tell you the treatments for hands and medicine, according to the accomplishment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and how they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	Wounds are made by the thrusting of a spear, cutting with swords and knives, or arrows, lances, or shafts, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	What are done according to the laws of the body, such as wounds that fall on the neck, or head, or belly, or liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the cure for each wound, and I will begin with the simple wounds of the head, because memories will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	When a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, be careful if it is due to an arrow or similar things, and the skin is entirely torn and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	And you doubt the draining of an abscess hot: if it makes blood come out from the head itself, even a little bit of blood from the wound, and the drainage is contrary to the damaged part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And the patient should purge himself of wine and thick foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	If he does not want to drain, let his food be reduced, and do not drink wine, nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And place on the wound, if hot abscess comes, cotton soaked in rose oil only, or in vinegar.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no abscess hot, put on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and it is not moved by air or powder, I will say a little later what the powder is;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the fire has moved it (the wound), put some ointments on it until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like the size of a sword and its lips cannot be brought together by tension, bring them together by suturing, as I will explain for abdominal wounds by suturing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed to the bone, festers, and does not hold firmly, press it; then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Instruct the patient to eat large meats such as boiled heads (testes) and wheat, also like pulses, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or suspect rotten flesh, without reaching the bone, press the entire thing, and pour hot liquid on it, then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein without a cord, and it cannot be stopped with medicines, you should tie it off; and if you find the artery dislocated, bind it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if that doesn't work, cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if the wounds are small and simple, the cure is easy; put this powder on it so that the arse moves it.

et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And then bind it tightly, and leave it to heal by itself if it does not swell; because one does not remove the medicine until it is healed.

de la plaie dou col	Of the wound of the neck.
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If a wound comes or is in the neck and it is simple without any difference from that of the head, but if the nerves of the neck or the artery are severed.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerves, there is no other remedy but to let them be and not apply any binding, for it harms the nerves and makes them retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And place nothing cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and the continuation of these is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but let the medicine be warm, like boiled water with sweet oil added to it, and boiled again in sweet water.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other stones of this kind, and always kept moist.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is large, then cut it and bind it with strips, until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and swollen with pus, pierce or puncture it (the wound) lower.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	If the artery is cut and bleeding occurs, stop it (the bleeding), tie it, and cauterize if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the spine in the throat (or windpipe) is cut or pierced, the food passage must be kept clear.
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	If the heart is near the neck of the throat, do not touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then let it come naturally and leave it for some days, then cure it with hot poultices until it is healed.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	If the wound presses on the bone, squeeze it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	If there are pieces of bone, remove them all if you can, and leave the rest until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And let the joints be dislocated and aligned.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle the powder that I have said on it.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	If there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a wound from a spear or knife, and the wound is deep, look to see if it has any pus discharge as the patient complains: then know that the wound is fatal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep, and it is all fresh blood, do not put any powder on it immediately or tie it up for the blood that disperses too much;
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and return to the patient's heart, and open the wound;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply an attracting ointment, and let it stay for two times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you do not have an ointment, put in the wound old cotton to draw out moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and make the patient rest on the wound for three days or four, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if there is no spasm or bad tremors of the heart and no drawing from the entrails.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good positions, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Apply the remedy and other treatments, as long as he is healthy;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	If it cannot heal, and if an abscess forms, then know that there is a fistula; treat it as needed.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	If the wound is from sword or knife incision and it is simple (not compounded), whether on the front or back, treat what is in front of it;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it is large, stitch it up; if it is small, powder it, and if it is embedded in the bone and has broken into pieces, either sew up the wound or draw out the fragments if they are exposed.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not exposed, let the wound drain, align the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on various limbs, judgement is made according to what we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	Breaking of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The breaking of the belly is great, medium, and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a large wound, the intestines sometimes protrude or the nerves of the intestines, due to which the insertion takes place.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worse than a large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Because more points are put into [the intestines], if they are not put in one by one.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines inflate quickly when they feel the heat, and more points enter them.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and for this reason it is better to stitch the midline wound, because it is better to sew the inflamed intestines in their place rather than others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the abdominal incision is according to four methods:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common joints occur in the abdomen joint.
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the joints of other wounds on the body and two other joints specific to those wounds are common to other wounds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Moreover, they are more appropriate with the abdomen joint, and I shall say one and explain it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and any internal organ protrudes from it,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And great care is required when resetting [something], this can be done in one of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or by the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to the cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	Moisten a sponge or a piece of cloth in cold water only,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	cook in squiant and cyper and pepper,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and stretch the intestine until the swelling is removed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And sometimes this wine restrains, and is boiled to dilute.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	When you see the swelling separate, if the intestines are cooked with too much or bad water,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for by this, the entry is closed almost completely;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, then make a small wound with the instrument used to treat hemorrhoids.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first treatment is cooked meat,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	we should not cut it unnecessarily;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And this is the instrument to cut with:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	Slice into it deeply along the curve and not across, and look at its shape here:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is widened, and the intestines burst out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	Put it back to its natural shape in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	If you can, for it is necessary.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide, and it is in the part beneath the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	make the patient lie on his back.
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and raise his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	if it is in the part beneath the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	if he sets his head and feet higher than the parts below.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and similarly, if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	If the broken part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus it should be applied to what I say in large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use what is appropriate;
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have between your hands a kind and compassionate minister who touches the entire wound with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	And hold the lips together;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common method of stitching (or suturing);
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you take a needle or several, according to the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	Then leave the edge of the wound a distance of two fingers (approximately one inch), and insert a needle with a single strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce the two shoulder blades with the two shoulder bones (ribs).
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is under the skin inside, as long as you are making it penetrate from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	And assemble the four shoulder bones together.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	Then tie a double thread around the needle of two parts (two threads).
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	Then assemble the two shoulders of the wound facing each other,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and leave one finger's width in space, and insert another needle.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue to do so according to the number of needles needed,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	As long as the entire wound is held closed;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	And the needles be medium-sized, neither too fine nor too thick.
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because the thin needles pierce all the skin, and the large ones cannot enter properly:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because they should be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	And it is not advisable to push the needles too far into the flesh and skin.
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so as not to open and pierce the wound before the suture.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	Then hold the heads of the needles, so that they do not prick the patient while sleeping.
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	And he puts tents or bandages on the head of arrows to keep it steady.
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leaves them until the wound is healed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	And this way of stitching arrows is more suitable for small wounds.
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	For he thrusts a needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second suture is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and you must gather together two shoulder blades and two rib bones with a needle having one strong middle thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced these bones all four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then remove the needle from the part where you started, in the manner one cuts meat.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place a space between each joint with the thickness of a hen's eggshell;
ceste costure sevent li home,	This joint is for the man,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	And I sew a wound which a man had or belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which was pierced by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than one palm wide,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and it exposed the intestines about two palms in length,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	And the wound was within the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I put back the intestine after it had been out for 24 hours.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound healed up to 15 days, and it was cured, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	The monk had judged that he would die, but this was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	And do not treat it with ointment, for I was in one place where none were found, nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And apply old cotton twice a day on the wound and wash it with water of honey until it is healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper ways of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and thrust it from the outer part towards the inner one until it reaches.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced through the core straight on straight, then take out the needle where its head was or where you had inserted the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and make it pierce from the inner part towards the outer one until it reaches.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the understanding of this stitch is that you sew as pelts are made by a tanner,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And you leave the suture open on one side, and close it on the other, until the stitches are all completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of suturing, as Galen calls it,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	it is similar to what anyone does when joining two natural parts together,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	And apply one of the cheeks of the jaw to the other cheek in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	Insert a needle or cheek of the mirror near that side, and only pierce it through there.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	leave the two cheeks of the jaw.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and pierce it from the outer part to the inner one.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	2 shoulders of the breastplate [or armor]
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then make a hole in one and the other of the exterior part up to that within, in 2 other shoulders of the cuirass [or armor] on the opposite side.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the manner of sewing and the most common one.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one contradicts it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One must sew the stomach with two needles, each containing thread.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one should push one needle from one side, and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew corsets.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	And know that when the incision is inside the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	The sewing is more difficult than other parts of the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments of the wound are as follows, similar to the judgments of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is when you find the fresh wound full of blood, just as the arrow moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if you reinsert the intestines and sew them up; then put powder made from charcoal on top,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	And if the arm has been moved, place some ointment on it while the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	Thread the sutures and sew them together with the needle;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as usual, until it is healed;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you have no medicine, place it immediately as soon as it begins to emit pus, old cotton.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it two times a day until it is healthy.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need any other medicine in many situations when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt whether the wound will spread to the main members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	It is necessary that you soften flax lightly in warm oil, or in rose oil.
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the sores, and under the saddlebags (bandages).
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	if there is pain or putrefaction in the belly, and this often happens,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if the cluster of black wine is hot, and especially when putrefaction reaches the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce within, know that when it is the large intestines, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The 'jeun' intestine cannot heal when perforated.
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is because of the wounds in them, and because of the subtlety of the whole body, and its proximity to nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the suture jumps out from the wound, replace it in the same manner as the intestine while it is fresh.
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it becomes old and turns black, you should lie the affected area so that blood does not flow from it.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	for there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the ligament.
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and hang the two heads on the side of the wound away from the extraction, so that when the sinews fall, the wound will be opened.
de la routure dou boueil	of the rupture of the bladder
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	it can be restored in some men,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen that a man was pierced or wounded by a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	And the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and became ulcerated and turned into a fistula, and in it there was exudation and flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated him according to what I knew, and did not stop refining until he was healthy, and the wounds closed up.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I see it sewn up, I feared that the patient has ill in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and he had no illness, but stayed in better condition, and ate and drank;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and the experimentalists said that when there is a small wound in the intestines, it should be sewn up in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take large clamps, then gather the lips of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	And when the convulsions have opened the mouth, place it on the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that it draws its mouth up;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then hold the head firmly so that he cannot loosen it.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then put another convulsion in this manner as before, until the wound is completely seized;
et cout la plaie.	And dress (or bandage) the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If the head swells in the intestines and brings no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and it can be tied with a thin string cut from the intestine of an animal.
en teil maniere:	In such a manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take this thread of intestine that is very thin,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie it to the head of this thin thread (or twist of linen).\]
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then thread the cord through the needle, sew the intestine and tie it in the wound.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this method of stitching tremors is not stronger than by way of faith and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	If the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the small intestines, there is no remedy or health, unless by subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula or that it is
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, when it heals, is universally called "fistula."
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and indeed, when it opens up and becomes hollow.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the truth, a hard and white swelling where no pain is felt,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it is swollen like the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And sometimes in a clear jump, and other times in a thick bow.
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Sometimes narrow, and other times quite wide.
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I have spoken about it in the section on wounds, that any wound which is not healed and there is no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	This is only through one of the four causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	or through the thinness of blood or body;
ou por sa malice;	or through its corruption:
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh within, and above the lips, which does not allow flesh to grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	When there is too much swelling;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	when the limb is pushed out (dislocated), and the matter is of bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	when the medicine is not good for the treatment.
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	because corruption is a type of plague;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	For the property of the region, digestion is slow, health delayed, and it naturally swells.
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	there are veins or bones
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, signs, and remedies for medicines in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I shall tell you the cure for fistula made by handwork.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that a fistula occurs in all members of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that come from large veins, arteries, and nerves.
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the bladder, intestines, bladder, or ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or in the spine of the back, or in any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	And if it [the dislocation] affects the principal member's property, and similar joints.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	All such fistulas are of grave healing, and there is nothing but labor and ignorance.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is any fistula that does not reach up to the level I mentioned, and you have faith in the cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And you may recognize it, if you take a tent of honey or iron, if the vein is straight, then pierce it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the vein is twisted, seek with a thin probe for it,
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because the probe bends around the twists;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	if the vein is severely damaged and you cannot find it with probes,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	if the hernia occurs through one of the perforations,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	for moisture cuts from one perforation to another and cleanses it;
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then carefully excise it to the extent of your skill, knowing if there is bone or nerve, and whether it is fully covered.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient carefully where he feels the pain when you press on it, and at what location.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	And when you truly know the location where it is, and if it is far from a joint, nerve, artery or vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in one of the places that I have told you, if the shoulder follows what I have told you,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and remove the rotten flesh and corrupt cartilage that are inside.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then heal it until it is healed,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	And if the fistula is correctly penetrated straight through, it must be sealed off as deeply as possible.
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	Then place dampened bandages soaked in a hot medicinal solution inside the fistula and push them to the tip of the fistula.
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine removes the excess that remains at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then apply ointment made with pure lard, until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	And if it is not healthy through this, cauterize it as we have said,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	and if the bone is rotten due to the abscess, break it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve does not affect major limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	and if the bone is exposed and there is corruption and blackness, scrape it until all the corruption is removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat harmful things until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	And if not healed, then bend as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	know that you are not going to the fountain:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	remove and dig deep until you reach the bottom,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	And remove all the corruption, then restore its place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus purified, it is well.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the corruption is too deep, that you cannot reach it;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other remedy but to let it heal on its own.
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	And if there is a small bone corrupted, and you can pull it with the pliers,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if extraction with an instrument is suitable for this,
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are many bones, pull them all out, do not leave any one.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if the moisture opposes you and there is no mistake or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	If hot and moist water and fat (or lard) are applied, and the bones are freed.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, apply something healing-balm to the wound.
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and let it remain until the flesh is swollen around the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	and then they will have more easily removed the bones;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	And if it is a large bone, such as of the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	then scrape off the corruption only to the extent that the blackness is entirely removed,
puis restoure la plaie;	then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	if there is a large part of the corruption and it reaches the bone marrow;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	If it is necessary to be cut open and covered until corruption occurs, and then it should be healed until it is closed;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	And I will tell you about a fistula that happened to one man in his leg,
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	so that you may take it as an example and help in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was a young man about thirty years old who had pain in his leg due to an internal cause that came from within the body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	Until substances came to the leg, and a large abscess broke out, without any reason to open [it].
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but they opened it anyway due to their foolishness, causing the abscess to burst open.
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	and they bled a great deal, and it became a fistula, and many died due to diarrhea and moisture of the body.
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and they both sought cures for two years, but there was no skilled surgeon among them.
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	as long as I was called upon, and saw his leg and the medications with which he was being treated
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and that which ran through the wounds with great force;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	and the youth's body became red, and had a yellowish hue.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I pitched a tent in one of the wounds, and then sought all the wounds,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	And I found that they come toward each other from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	Then I hurried and cut into one of the wounds until I discovered a part of the bone,
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	and I found it rotten and pierced, and the corruption went to the bone within;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I seemed to see the rotten bone, and thought that there was no other corruption except what I left behind;
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And begins to treat the wound with salves for long times, but cannot heal.
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	Then again it is reinforced and the bone is exposed as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	And found a continuous corruption in the bone, and burned it, then left it to heal and tried to mend the place.
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	But I could not heal more than covering a palm of the bone and draining all its marrow.
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	Then restore it with medicines; it heals and hardens quickly.
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	and should not begin the work again except for the weakness of the patient, who could not endure.
et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and because of the fear of death I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	Because it bled frequently but healed completely.
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	And in its place, a hard growth arises from the bone, and it was well-composed and had no harm or counteraction of any kind, neither at its edge nor its arrival.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, it must be treated thus:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	Take a ligature and bind the end of the broken bone.
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	And command anyone to stretch it upwards;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	And put another thread of coarser linen than the first one, and tie it above the flesh that is over the bone,
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	and stretch the head, so that you pull out the rotten flesh beneath it.
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	and expose the skin on the side where you want to be, so that the skin does not puncture the flesh;
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And put a splint or a plank under the bone to cover the corrupt flesh.
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	And it should be as much as one can see and feel the corruption, and also another time.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie,	If the bone is corrupt and does not open, and the corruption is in the middle or a part of it,
si descuevre la char toute; puis met .i. tison desoz,	If you uncover all the flesh, then put a splint underneath,
et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption .i. poc, si com nos avons dit;	And, let the corruption extend from one part to another, and let it be equal in length to the length of the corruption, i.e., finger span, as we have said.
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	If the corruption is in the joint, strike the corrupted joint and break the bone on the other side.
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	And if the corruption extends between two joints, there is no remedy but to strike it.
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	If the corruption is at the wrist of the hand or the ankle of the foot, it is a very difficult thing to treat.
mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	But nonetheless, you must inquire about that corruption, how it opens itself;
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	and clean it in all ways that you can, but ensure the vein or nerve do not oppose you;
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous,	and know that the incision and saws for cutting these bones are many, according to the position of the bones and their appearance;
et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	and their thickness and subtlety, and their largeness and smallness, and hardness;
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	And for this reason, it is necessary to prepare an instrument for every kind of work.
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art,	And know that the work will show you the instrument you will need, according to the knowledge of this craft,
et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	and the testimony of the ways of diseases;
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	if you think about the instrument that you need, according to what is necessary.
dou feu	hot fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The heads may fall out due to internal causes, or due to external ones;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie,	and when you have given the remedy for this corruption through the use of medicines, and it does not benefit at all,
si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient,	it is necessary to cover that member up to the level where the corruption comes,
si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	The patient escapes from death by this means or by the greater malice of the defect of a limb.
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu,	and the signs are that the limb turns black as if it had been burned by fire.
et porrist aprés la noiror, puis va celle corrosions de membre em membre,	and after the blackness comes the corrosion of one member after another.
et prent par tout le cors; si te haste dou coper,	and take the whole body by hand; hasten to cover.
et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans,	and if it is by the striking of some venomous beasts, such as sea scorpions and snakes and similar.
se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	if the corruption is at the top of the thumb, strike it, and do not give it any space to come up to the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it comes up to the hand, strike it at the joint, so that the corruption does not come up to the arm;
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute; et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors,	And if it comes to the arm, strike at the edge; and if it passes the edge, it is death.
et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	And no remedy is useful for it except its quantity of virtue.
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet: s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	And thus do as when the corruption comes or peels: if it comes at the first joint, then scrape after the other joint;
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	and if it comes in peeling, then scrape the whole peel.
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	If it rises in the leg, then scrape at the knee joint.
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	And if it comes above the knee, there is no other remedy for the patient but death.
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz,	and the manner of covering or healing the member is to bind it above and below.
et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont,	stretch one minister one of the lower bonds, and another minister the other bond upward.
et tu dessevre la char qui est entre les .ij. liiens a .i. spatumile large, tant que li os soit descovers;	and you cut through the flesh that is between the two bonds with a spatula-shaped tool, until the bone is exposed.
puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part .i. drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain,	Then take linen cloth or wool, and place one on each side, so that the wool does not touch the healthy flesh.
et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	And the patient comes to you with another wound or abscess dressed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment,	And if blood flow occurs when you are working, then cauterize the place immediately.
ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans; puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie,	or you put some restraining powders on it; then return to your medicine until it is completed,
puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then bind the member with a firm ligature, and cure it until it heals;
et je te conterai k’il avint a .i. home en som piet:	and I will tell you what happened to one man in my opinion:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu,	a man had a black spot which seemed burned by fire,
et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	And the burn started first in his lower leg, until it consumed all of the lower leg;
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	And when a person sees the corrosion, he pierces it with copper, and it becomes healthy.
et lonc tens aprés li revint li corrosion ou doi de la main, et il vint a moi,	For a long time after the corrosion recedes or from one hand it comes to me.
et je li mis sus choses repercussives aprés la mundification dou cors, et ne pot cesser li corrosions;	and I placed him on things that caused it to recur after the purification of the body, but the corrosion could not cease.
et il vot que je li copasse la main, et je ne vou, que je avoie esperance de repercuter la matiere;	And you ask me to cut off his hand, but I have no hope of recurrence of the matter.
et doutai ausi que se je tailloie sa main, qu’il ne morist,	And doubt also if I am to cut his hand, he will not die,
car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible; et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre,	for the virtue of man was weak; and he lost all hope and returned to his earth,
et se hasta de coper sa main, et fut sanez;	and pierced with a copper sword, he was healed;
et je n’ai ceu conteit fuers que por ceu c’on faice autreteil, s’on en a mestier.	and I have not heard this story except that it is done differently if it is needed.
Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	Aposteme sometimes comes in a charnut place and stays for so long that it causes a great swelling of the body.
et puis ront et perce, et en saut li bowe, et demoure li leus vuis, ausi com uns vasselz;	And then it runs and pierces through, causing the body to jump, and keeps the limbs open like a knight.
et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com .i. drapelz deliiez,	And the skin that is above it is as thin as one layer of undyed cloth.
et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain»,	and will not run to the bone or nerve, and such disease is called "sain".
et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	and is not called "fistula"
mais s’elle est si alongie qu’elle viegne jusc’a l’os em parfont, si est apelee «fistule»;	but if it is so long that it reaches the bone in full, then it is called "fistula";
et li cuire si est que tu cope celui cuir tout entor, et meismement quant il est subtilz, ausi com uns drapelz;	and the surgeon must cut all around the skin, and likewise when it is thin, as with a cloth;
et ne s’aert mie por sa corruption.	and does not heal due to its corruption.
Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont,	And if you have certainty that the flesh hardens, and the corruption is not yet complete,
et li cuir est espés de char, si le cure de clistere ensi:	and the flesh thickens with pus, cure it with a clysteris (enema) like this:
regarde se li seins est grans, et li bowe qui en ist est de puant odor,	observe if the breasts are swollen, and the sore in them smells of bad odor,
adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	Then apply the Egyptian medical ointment, which is made as follows:
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en .i. vassel au feu,	take asafoetida, oil, litharge, equally, and cook in one vessel over fire,
tant que li medicine soit rouge, et deviegne ausi espesse com miel;	let the mixture be red, and thicken like honey;
et puis pren de ceu selonc ta necessiteit, et le font en aigue et en miel,	take from this as needed, make it into water and honey,
et en clisterize lou sein, et estraint le pertus;	And in cauterizing the breast, apply pressure on the wound.
et laisse la medicine ens par .ij. houres, puis l’estrai en espreignant;	Leave the medicine for two hours, then remove it by pulling.
fai ce mout de fois, tant que li seins soit mondefiiez, et soit ostee li puor;	Do this repeatedly until the breast is purified and the pus is removed.
et aucune fois est clisterizeis d’aigue de cendres,	And occasionally the breast is cauterized with ashes,
quant ceste medicine n’est presens, et est que tu preignes cendres de fust de vigne, et giete aigue desus,	When this medicine is absent, and you take vine charcoal ashes, and pour water over it.
puis la coule, et en clisterize, tant que tu saiches que li seins est bien mondez;	then wash, and anoint with ointment, until you know that the wound is healed.
et se li malaides ne le puet soffrir, ne la medicine egiptiaine ne l’aigue de cendres,	if the patient cannot bear it, or the Egyptian medicine or water of ashes do not help.
si le clisterize d’aigue et de miel ou il ait un poc de litargire broiet;	if you anoint with oil, honey, and a little bit of litharge powdered.
ou tu la clistirize de miel et de vin melleit, que li mielz ait proprieteit de mundifiier et de laver,	or you anoint it with honey and sweet wine, as the honey has properties to cleanse and wash,
et li vins fait aerdre le sain;	and the wine makes the blood thicken;
et quant tu as ce fait, et tu as fiance que li seins est bien mundifiiez,	and when you have done this, and you are confident that the wound is well cleaned,
si le clisterize de ceu que fait naistre char en li,	If the clisterization of this one that causes growth of chaff within him,
et est que tu preignes emplaustre diafinit, et le font avec oile roset et en vin;	and you take a plaster made definite, and make it with rose oil and wine.
ou tu le clisterize d’aucunes medicines et d’oignemens, dont j’ai dit les proprietez ou traitier des oignemens;	or you clisterize it with some medicines and ointments, as I have said the properties or treatment of ointments.
et se li pertus dou sein est petis, et li cainne dou clistere n’i puet entrer,	if the wound of the breast is small, and the plaster of the clister cannot enter,
si l’eslarge d’un fer un poc, et met ens une tente de l’oignement egiptiein,	If a wound from a small sword is opened, put an Egyptian bandage on it.
ou oignement basilicon, tant k’il soit eslargiez;	or Basilicon ointment, until it is widened;
et se li plaie est trop large, si la cout et i laisse tant soulement .i. leu ou li clistere puisse entrer,	and if the wound is too wide, cut (or make) it so that only one inch or a clister can enter;
et se li pertus que giete bowe est au desus, si le cope ou plus bas leu que i est.	and if the hernia that protrudes above is in the lower part, push it down or lower than it is.
Car quant li bowe est en parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char;	For when the bow is fully drawn, do not let it catch char.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	and if you cannot cover the breast beneath as you see,
si appareille en tel maniere que li bowe corre au plus bas leu que i est,	arrange in such a way that the bow moves to the lowest point possible.
car quant li bowe est parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char	For when the bow is fully drawn, do not let it catch char.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	And if you cannot cover the chest underneath as you see,
si apareille en teil maniere: que li bowe corre legierement aval, et n’i lassier rien de la bowe;	and arrange in this manner: let the arm hang loosely downward, and do not leave anything from the arm;
et pren medicines consolidatives por mettre sor le sein,	and take consolidating medicines to put on the chest,
et estent sus .i. drapeil de lin que cuevre tout le sein;	and stretch out one linen cloth that covers the entire chest;
puis cope as forces endroit le pertus dou sein .i. poc plus large dou premier,	Then apply force to the puncture wound in the chest. That is, use a bandage larger than the first one.
pues estent oignement souef sus .i. autre drapel selonc la quantiteit dou pertus,	Then anoint the wound with oil or another cloth according to the size of the wound.
et le met sus le pertus dou sein por aligier la bowe, et n’oster mie le grant drapeil fuers que aprés maint jor une fois;	and place it on the chest wound to heal the bone, and do not remove the large cloth unless after several days.
et celui qui est sor le pertus dou sein, oste sovent por oster la bowe,	and he who is over the chest wound, remove it frequently to draw out the bone.
et saiches ceu que corra de la bowe, se c’est venin ou poc ou assez, ou digeste, ou indigeste;	And know what runs from the bowel, whether it is poison or pus or enough or digested, or undigested;
et pren warde se li patiens sent dolor ou nom, et s’il i a aposteme ou non,	and take care if the patient feels pain or not, and if there is an abscess or not,
et quant ta medicine s’est en teil maniere estendue et tu vois la nature que saut sus le pertus dou sein,	and when your remedy has been stretched out in this manner and you see the boil rising on the breast;
si saiches que li seins s’aert ja, et aproche li santez;	If you know that breasts always swell, approach them with health.
et puis le deslie le matin, ou le tier jor, et quant tu delies la plaie,	and in the morning or at midday, when you are dislocating the wound.
si chainge .i. autre drapeil, et renovele l’oignement.	and change one other dressing, and renew the treatment.
Et se li seins giete bowe indigeste aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie.	And if the breasts are swollen improperly after many days, know that breasts do not always swell.
Et se venins subtilz cort aprés lonc tens, si ne te desperer mie de la santeit,	And if subtle poisonous worms appear after a long time, do not despair of health.
car li santez aproche. Car il i a homes cui tarde enjanremens de char en ses plaies, et de ces que font le contraire;	for the healing approaches. For there are people whose wounds grow cold in their injuries and those who make it worse.
et se bowe indigeste saut dou sein aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie;	and if the belly swells with excessive gas after many days, know that the stomach does not empty.
et se li seins tarde d’aerdre, et est porloigniez, si ajoste medicines sechans moistes en substance et seches en vertut,	And if the breast delays in healing and is extended, place drying medications containing moist substances but dry in properties.
si com oignement diafinit, car il i a grant partie de vitriole, et c’est li derriene medicine;	Similarly, define it as an ointment since it contains much vitriol, and this is the final medication;
